===
square(a) ^ size(a, 3)
Build a 3 block by 3 block square.
square(b) ^ size(b, 3) ^ square(a) ^ left(b, a)
Next, create a square with sides of block length 3 to the left of the first square.
square(b) ^ square(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ lower_right(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ left_side(a, d, 0) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w2, w1)
Ensure that the lower right corner of this square is next to the first square's upper left corner.

===
column(a) ^ height(a, 3)
First, construct a column using 3 blocks.
column(b) ^ height(b, 3) ^ column(a) ^ top(b, a)
After that, construct a column of size 3 to the top of the column.
column(b) ^ column(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ lower_left(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ upper_left(a, d) ^ spatial-rel(north, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the bottom end of this column is next to the top end of the first column.
rectangle(e) ^ height(e, 4) ^ width(e, 2) ^ column(b) ^ left(e, b)
Finally, form a rectangle that is 2 blocks wide and 4 blocks tall to the left of the second column.
rectangle(e) ^ column(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_right(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ left_side(b, g, 1) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the rectangle's upper right corner is next to the second row of the second column.

Make sure that the second row of the rectangle is adjacent to the row's left end.

Next, construct a vertical line with 3 blocks to the left of the rectangle.
column(b) ^ rectangle(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_right(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ upper_left(a, d) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the top end of the vertical line is adjacent to the upper left corner of the rectangle.
rectangle(e) ^ height(e, 2) ^ width(e, 3) ^ column(b) ^ top(e, b)
Finally, form a rectangle with a width of 3 blocks and a height of 2 blocks to the top of the vertical line.

Make sure that the lower left corner of the new rectangle is next to the vertical line's top end.

===
square(a) ^ size(a, 4)
First, form a 4 block by 4 block square.
rectangle(b) ^ height(b, 2) ^ width(b, 3) ^ square(a) ^ left(b, a)
Next, build a rectangle that is 2 blocks tall and 3 blocks wide to the left of the square.
rectangle(b) ^ square(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_right(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ left_side(a, d, 2) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the rectangle's upper right corner is adjacent to the third row of the square.
column(e) ^ height(e, 3) ^ square(a) ^ right(e, a)
Finally, create a column with 3 blocks to the right of the rectangle.
column(e) ^ square(a) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_left(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ upper_right(a, g) ^ spatial-rel(east, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the column's top end is next to the square's upper right corner.

Make sure that the upper left corner of the rectangle is in line with the vertical line's bottom end.
rectangle(e) ^ height(e, 2) ^ width(e, 4) ^ rectangle(b) ^ bottom(e, b)
Finally, construct a rectangle that is 2 blocks tall and 4 blocks wide to the bottom of the first rectangle.
rectangle(e) ^ rectangle(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_left(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ lower_left(b, g) ^ spatial-rel(south, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the new rectangle's upper left corner is in line with the first rectangle's lower left corner.

Ensure that the lower right corner of the square is next to the row's left end.

Make sure that the second row of the rectangle is next to the right end of the row.

Finally, form a horizontal line with 3 blocks to the top of the rectangle.

Make sure that the horizontal line's right end is adjacent to the upper right corner of the rectangle.

column(a) ^ height(a, 4)
First, form a column using 4 blocks.
rectangle(b) ^ height(b, 4) ^ width(b, 2) ^ column(a) ^ bottom(b, a)
Then, construct a rectangle with a width of 2 blocks and a height of 4 blocks to the bottom of the column.
rectangle(b) ^ column(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_left(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ lower_left(a, d) ^ spatial-rel(south, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the upper left corner of the rectangle is adjacent to the bottom end of the column.
rectangle(e) ^ height(e, 2) ^ width(e, 3) ^ rectangle(b) ^ left(e, b)
Finally, form a rectangle that is 3 blocks wide and 2 blocks tall to the left of the first rectangle.
rectangle(e) ^ rectangle(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_right(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ left_side(b, g, 2) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that this rectangle's upper right corner is aligned with the third row of the first rectangle.

Next, build a 2 block by 2 block square to the bottom of the rectangle.
square(b) ^ rectangle(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_right(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ bottom_side(a, d, 0) ^ spatial-rel(south, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the square's upper right corner is next to the rectangle's lower left corner.

Finally, form a column of size 3 to the bottom of the square.
column(e) ^ square(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_left(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ lower_left(b, g) ^ spatial-rel(south, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the column's top end is in line with the lower left corner of the square.

Next, create a rectangle with a width of 3 blocks and a height of 2 blocks to the bottom of the square.
rectangle(b) ^ square(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_left(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ bottom_side(a, d, 1) ^ spatial-rel(south, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the upper left corner of the rectangle is next to the lower right corner of the square.
rectangle(e) ^ height(e, 3) ^ width(e, 2) ^ square(a) ^ left(e, a)
Finally, build a rectangle that is 2 blocks wide and 3 blocks tall to the left of the first rectangle.
rectangle(e) ^ square(a) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_right(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ left_side(a, g, 1) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the upper right corner of the new rectangle is next to the square's lower left corner.

Then, create a rectangle that is 2 blocks wide and 3 blocks tall to the left of the square.

Make sure that the upper right corner of the rectangle is in line with the square's upper left corner.
row(e) ^ width(e, 4) ^ rectangle(b) ^ top(e, b)
Finally, construct a horizontal line of size 4 to the top of the rectangle.
row(e) ^ rectangle(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ bottom_side(e, f, 1) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ upper_left(b, g) ^ spatial-rel(north, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the second column of the horizontal line is adjacent to the rectangle's upper left corner.

Construct a rectangle that is 3 blocks tall and 4 blocks wide.
rectangle(b) ^ height(b, 3) ^ width(b, 4) ^ rectangle(a) ^ right(b, a)
After that, build a 4 by 3 rectangle to the right of the first rectangle.
rectangle(b) ^ rectangle(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_left(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ right_side(a, d, 1) ^ spatial-rel(east, 0, w2, w1)
Ensure that the new rectangle's upper left corner is adjacent to the second row of the first rectangle.

Then, build a rectangle with a width of 4 blocks and a height of 2 blocks to the left of the rectangle.
rectangle(b) ^ rectangle(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_right(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ left_side(a, d, 1) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w2, w1)
Make sure that the upper right corner of this rectangle is adjacent to the second row of the first rectangle.
square(e) ^ size(e, 2) ^ rectangle(b) ^ left(e, b)
Finally, create a 2 block by 2 block square to the left of the second rectangle.
square(e) ^ rectangle(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ upper_right(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ left_side(b, g, 1) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the square's upper right corner is next to the lower left corner of the second rectangle.

Make sure that the lower right corner of the rectangle is next to the upper left corner of the square.

Finally, create a 3 by 3 square to the right of the rectangle.

Make sure that this square's upper left corner is adjacent to the lower right corner of the first square.

Make sure that the right end of this row is next to the second column of the first row.

Finally, build a column of size 4 to the left of the second row.
column(e) ^ row(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ lower_right(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ lower_left(b, g) ^ spatial-rel(west, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the bottom end of the column is aligned with the second row's left end.

Next, construct a rectangle that is 2 blocks wide and 4 blocks tall to the bottom of the horizontal line.
rectangle(b) ^ row(a) ^ block(c) ^ location(w1) ^ block-location(c, w1) ^ upper_left(b, c) ^ block(d) ^ location(w2) ^ block-location(d, w2) ^ bottom_side(a, d, 3) ^ spatial-rel(south, 0, w2, w1)

square(e) ^ size(e, 3) ^ row(a) ^ top(e, a)
Finally, form a 3 by 3 square to the top of the rectangle.
square(e) ^ row(a) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ lower_right(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ top_side(a, g, 1) ^ spatial-rel(north, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the square's lower right corner is next to the second column of the horizontal line.

After that, form a rectangle with a width of 3 blocks and a height of 2 blocks to the left of the first rectangle.

Ensure that this rectangle's lower right corner is next to the upper left corner of the first rectangle.

Make sure that the new column's top end is next to the second row of the first column.

square(e) ^ size(e, 3) ^ row(b) ^ top(e, b)
Finally, build a 3 block by 3 block square to the top of the horizontal line.
square(e) ^ row(b) ^ block(f) ^ location(w3) ^ block-location(f, w3) ^ lower_left(e, f) ^ block(g) ^ location(w4) ^ block-location(g, w4) ^ top_side(b, g, 1) ^ spatial-rel(north, 0, w4, w3)
Make sure that the lower left corner of the new square is next to the second column of the horizontal line.

Make sure that this square's upper right corner is next to the lower right corner of the rectangle.
